commit 03acf2fa2bf46b5d53a51bffd9cdb99781b25550
Author: Matte Noble <me@mattenoble.com>
Date:   Wed Apr 3 15:00:05 2019 -0700

    feat(app-platform): Expose SentryApp author (#12622)
    
    Developers need to be able to specify who created and maintains Sentry
    Apps.
    
    This change allows them to input them and exposes them thoughout the API
    where necessary.

@@ -69,6 +52,25 @@ class SentryAppSerializer(Serializer):

+    def __init__(self, instance=None, *args, **kwargs):
+        self.instance = instance
+        super(SentryAppSerializer, self).__init__(*args, **kwargs)
+
+    def validate_name(self, attrs, source):
+        if not attrs.get('name'):
+            return attrs
+
+        queryset = SentryApp.with_deleted.filter(slug=slugify(attrs['name']))
+
+        if self.instance:
+            queryset = queryset.exclude(id=self.instance.id)
+
+        if queryset.exists():
+            raise ValidationError(
+                u'Name {} is already taken, please use another.'.format(attrs['name'])
+            )
+        return attrs
+
     def validate_events(self, attrs, source):

             return attrs
